      <script type="text/javascript" src="/slider/jquery.min.js"></script> 
      <script type="text/javascript">// <![CDATA[
$(document).ready(function() {

	//Set Default State of each portfolio piece
	$(".paging").show();
	$(".paging a:first").addClass("active");

		
	//Get size of images, how many there are, then determine the size of the image reel.
	var imageWidth = $(".window").width();
	var imageSum = $(".image_reel img").size();
	var imageReelWidth = imageWidth * imageSum;
	
	//Adjust the image reel to its new size
	$(".image_reel").css({'width' : imageReelWidth});
	
	//Paging + Slider Function
	rotate = function(){	
		var triggerID = $active.attr("rel") - 1; //Get number of times to slide
		var image_reelPosition = triggerID * imageWidth; //Determines the distance the image reel needs to slide

		$(".paging a").removeClass('active'); //Remove all active class
		$active.addClass('active'); //Add active class (the $active is declared in the rotateSwitch function)

		
		//Slider Animation
		$(".image_reel").animate({ 
			left: -image_reelPosition
		}, 500 );
		
	}; 
	
	//Rotation + Timing Event
	rotateSwitch = function(){		
		play = setInterval(function(){ //Set timer - this will repeat itself every 3 seconds
			$active = $('.paging a.active').next();
			if ( $active.length === 0) { //If paging reaches the end...
				$active = $('.paging a:first'); //go back to first

			}
			rotate(); //Trigger the paging and slider function
		}, 16000); //Timer speed in milliseconds (3 seconds)
	};
	
	rotateSwitch(); //Run function on launch
	
	//On Hover
	$(".image_reel a").hover(function() {
		clearInterval(play); //Stop the rotation
	}, function() {
		rotateSwitch(); //Resume rotation
	});	
	
	//On Click
	$(".paging a").click(function() {	
		$active = $(this); //Activate the clicked paging
		//Reset Timer
		clearInterval(play); //Stop the rotation
		rotate(); //Trigger rotation immediately
		rotateSwitch(); // Resume rotation
		return false; //Prevent browser jump to link anchor
	});	
	
});
// ]]></script>

      <p>&nbsp;</p> 
      <ul> 
       <li> <h4>Chancellor Kim A. Wilcox's &quot;Campus of Respect&quot; Letter to the Community</h4> 
        <blockquote>
         At the University of California, Riverside, our students, faculty, staff, and guests represent myriad personal experiences and values that grow out of both differences and often unrecognized similarities in culture, background, and outlooks. 
         <a href="/campusrespect2013.pdf" target="_blank">Read the full message here.</a>
        </blockquote> </li> 
       <li> <h4>UCR Strategic Plan: A Path to Preeminence</h4> 
        <blockquote>
         <a href="http://strategicplan.ucr.edu/documents/UCR%202020%20-%20Final.pdf" target="_blank">The strategic action plan</a> serves UCR over the course of the next decade, guiding the campus to assume its position among the top research universities in the nation. To fulfill its vision, the campus has identified four overarching strategic goals: academic excellence, access, diversity, and engagement.
        </blockquote> </li> 
       <li> <h4>Chancellor's Diversity Education Program: Making Excellence Inclusive (MEI)</h4> 
        <blockquote>
         UCR established the Diversity Education &amp; Leadership Initiative (DELI) in 2008 to promote, coordinate and oversee diversity activities on the campus. Since that time DELI has established the Chancelor's Diversity Education Program: Making Excellent Inclusive (MEI).
        </blockquote> </li> 
       <li> <h4>UC Riverside Lauded for Diversity, Value in the U.S. News &amp; World Report's 2014 Best&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Colleges Guide</h4> 
        <blockquote>
         The University of California, Riverside has once-again been recognized as a &quot;Best Value School&quot; and was lauded for its diversity in the U.S. News and World Report's 2014 Best Colleges Guide.&nbsp; 
         <a href="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/17243" target="_blank">Read more here.</a>
        </blockquote> </li> 
       <li> <h4>UC Riverside Named a Military Friendly School for Third Consecutive Year</h4> 
        <blockquote>
         For the third year in a row, the University of California, Riverside has been recognized as a Military Friendly School by Victory Media. The honor recognizes the university for its efforts to assist America's military service members and veterans as students. 
         <a href="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/17352" target="_blank">Read more here.</a>
         <a class="scroll" href="#top"><span class="top_page">top</span></a>
        </blockquote> </li> 
      </ul>

    <div class="list-land" id="content"> 
     <!-- Main hero unit for a primary marketing message or call to action --> 
     <div class="row"> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <h1 class="page-header">Financial Services and Controls</h1> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <!-- Example row of columns --> 
     <div class="row-fluid"> 
      <div class="span4 hero-unit"> 
       <p>We provide systemwide banking and treasury services, faculty mortgage lending, and managed travel programs.</p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4">
       <p>Financial Services and Controls is responsible for systemwide financial services, cash management, financial controls and accountability. By aligning banking needs with appropriate service providers and managing vendor relationships (depository, disbursement, purchase card, travel card, merchant card), we strive to ensure optimal pricing and service.&nbsp;We also originate and service mortgage loans for nominated faculty and senior staff and develop, implement and operate the university's central travel management program.</p>
      </div> 
      <div class="span4"> 
       <div class="row-fluid dotted-bottom"> 
        <div class="span4 dept-head"> 
         <img alt="Daniel C. Sampson" src="_images/shot_44_dsampson_024.jpg" />
        </div> 
        <div class="span8"> 
         <p class="blue"> Daniel C. Sampson </p> 
         <p>Assistant Vice President</p> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row-fluid"> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon staff" href="staff/index.html">Staff Directory</a>
        </div> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon org" href="_files/fsc-org-chart.pdf">Org Chart</a>
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="row-fluid blustripe dept-unit"> 
      <h2 class="nobtm">DEPARTMENTS</h2> 
      <div class="row-fluid col5"> 
       <div class="span4"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/banking-treasury-services/index.html">Banking and Treasury Services</a> </h3> 
        <p>Provides systemwide guidance, expertise and leadership for banking and related services used in the administration of UC funds.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/banking-treasury-services/policies-guidelines/index.html">Policies and guidelines</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/banking-treasury-services/forms/index.html">Forms</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
       <div class="span4"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/central-travel-management/index.html">Central Travel Management</a> </h3> 
        <p>Supports and manages university travel, including development and implementation of the Connexxus system.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/central-travel-management/connexxus/booking-options.html">Booking options</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/central-travel-management/resources/travel-insurance--regulations/index.html">Travel insurance and regulations</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
       <div class="span4"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/loan-programs/index.html">Office of Loan Programs</a> </h3> 
        <p>Designs, delivers and manages mortgage lending products for the recruitment and retention of faculty and senior managers.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/loan-programs/loan-programs/mortgage-origination-program.html">Mortgage Origination Program (MOP)</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/loan-programs/resources/faqs-about-new-uc-home-loans.html">FAQs about new UC home loans</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="row less3 novrflw"> 
      <div class="span6 grybx"> 
       <h4>Contact us</h4> 
       <p> <br /> Financial Services and Controls<br /> University of California<br /> Office of the President<br /> 1111 Franklin Street, 10th Floor<br /> Oakland, CA 94607-5201<br /> </p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span6 grybx"> 
       <h4>UC InfoCenter</h4> 
       <p>The <a href="http://data.universityofcalifornia.edu/">UC InfoCenter</a> provides a repository of up-to-date and accessible data about the university, including:</p> 
       <img align="left" alt="Graph" height="85" src="/institutional-research/_images/graph.jpg" style="margin: 0px 20px 0px 0px;" vspace="0" width="85" /> 
       <p style="padding-left: 60px;">&gt;&nbsp;<a href="http://data.universityofcalifornia.edu/student/">Students</a><br /> &gt;&nbsp;<a href="http://data.universityofcalifornia.edu/finance/">Finance</a><br /> &gt;&nbsp;<a href="http://data.universityofcalifornia.edu/faculty-staff/">Faculty &amp; staff</a><br /> &gt;&nbsp;<a href="http://data.universityofcalifornia.edu/accountability/">Accountability</a></p> 
      </div>

      } else {

        // Google WaterMark Script
        $(function () {
            $("#txtGoogleSearch").each(function () {
                ToggleHint($(this)); // add class on page load to elements with "hintable" class
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").focus(function () {
                $(this).removeClass("GoogleWatermark"); // handle all focus hints
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").blur(function () {
                ToggleHint(this); // handle all blur hints
            });
        });

        function ToggleHint(obj) {
            if ($(obj).val() == '') { $(obj).addClass("GoogleWatermark"); };
        }
    </script>

     <img src="/Images/family.png" alt="" class="page-lead" /> 
     <div class="span-18 last"> 
      <h3>Families: Access Your Student's Records</h3> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-9"> 
      <span class="warning">Important:</span> 
      <ul class="orange-bullets"> 
       <li>UCR never gives private information out over the phone or by email (even with consent).</li> 
       <li><a href="http://www.growl.ucr.edu" target="_blank">Growl</a> is the online system students use to track their grades, view their transcripts, register for classes and view their financial statement of account.</li> 
      </ul> 
      <h3>Students Control Who Sees Their Information</h3> 
      <p>While you understandably have an interest in your child's academic, financial or disciplinary records, you need permission to access those records. Your student can grant you that permission in a few different ways. See our <a href="/registrar/privacy-ferpa/disclosure-policies.aspx">Disclosure Policies</a> for more details.</p> 
      <p>In general, sensitive information is only shared with the student’s consent, in a health or safety emergency or in accordance with another FERPA exception. </p> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-9 last"> 
      <div class="sidebar"> 
       <img src="/Images/folder.png" style="float: right; margin: 4px;" /> 
       <div class="title">
         FERPA Resources: 
       </div> 
       <ul> 
        <li><a href="http://www.ucop.edu/general-counsel/_files/ed-affairs/ferpa101.pdf" target="_new">UC FERPA 101</a></li> 
        <li><a href="http://www.ed.gov/policy/gen/guid/fpco/ferpa/index.html" target="_new">US Department of Education and FERPA</a></li> 
        <li><a href="http://policy.ucop.edu/doc/2710533/PACAOS-130" target="_new">UC FERPA Policy</a></li> 
        <li><a href="../privacy-ferpa/ucr-ferpa-policy.aspx">UCR FERPA Policy</a></li> 
        <li><a href="http://www.dol.gov/dol/ppii.htm" target="_new">US Protection of Personal Information Policies</a></li> 
        <li><a href="http://www2.ed.gov/policy/gen/guid/fpco/index.html" target="_new">US Department of Education Family Policy Compliance Office</a></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-18 last"> 
      <h3>Frequently Asked Questions</h3> 
      <br /> 
      <div class="accordion"> 
       <h4> <img src="/Images/square-bullet.png" alt="" /> How can I get a copy of my student's grades?</h4> 
       <div> 
        <ul> 
         <li>1. Your student can give that information directly (e.g. print or email you a copy of their records).</li> 
         <li>2. Your student can set you up as an “authorized user&quot; in their Growl account. <a href="http://vcsatest.ucr.edu/Registrar-Website/registrar/privacy-ferpa/disclosure-policies.aspx">See how.</a></li> 
        </ul> 
       </div> 
       <h4> <img src="/Images/square-bullet.png" alt="" /> I'm paying for my child's education, why can't I get a copy of their records?</h4> 
       <div> 
        <p>According to FERPA, a student’s records do not belong to the person paying for the student’s education – they belong to the student. Information is only shared with the student’s consent, in a health or safety emergency or pursuant to another FERPA exception. Your child may grant you permission to access their records in many ways. Please see our <a href="/registrar/privacy-ferpa/disclosure-policies.aspx">Disclosure Policies</a> for details. </p> 
       </div> 
       <h4> <img src="/Images/square-bullet.png" alt="" /> My student granted me access to Growl. Can you email a copy of his or her transcript?</h4> 
       <div> 
        <p>We never release confidential information over the phone or by email. See our Request a Transcript page for ways to obtain one. </p> 
       </div> 
       <h4> <img src="/Images/square-bullet.png" alt="" /> My student granted me access to Growl, what do I have permission to see? </h4> 
       <div> 
        <p>Through Growl, your student can set it up so you can see their billing statements, financial aid information, grades and class schedule. They can also request that email reminders (including billing reminders) are sent directly to your email account.</p> 
        <p>Your student can also use Growl to grant you permission to speak with <a href="http://finaid.ucr.edu/" target="_blank">Financial Aid</a>, <a href="http://housing.ucr.edu" target="_blank">Housing</a>, and <a href="http://www.sbs.ucr.edu/" target="_blank">Student Business Services</a> about your student’s financial account.</p> 
        <p>Growl authorization does not necessarily extend to other campus offices nor automatically grant you permission to discuss your child’s student record with the university.</p> 
        <p>Your student may also fill out a department-specific authorization forms if your Growl access isn’t getting you the information you need.</p> 
       </div> 
       <h4> <img src="/Images/square-bullet.png" alt="" /> Can’t I just fill out one form and have access to everything?</h4> 
       <div> 
        <p>UCR does not have a blanket release form covering the release of all student information to you. Release forms are generally very specific and students may be required to fill out department-specific authorization forms each time they request information be shared with you.</p> 
       </div> 
       <h4> <img src="/Images/square-bullet.png" alt="" /> Does my Growl authorization or FERPA allow me access to my student’s medical and counseling records?</h4> 
       <div> 
        <p>Not necessarily, unless it is an emergency. However, your student may be able to grant you access via specific release forms. Questions about medical records should be directed to the <a href="http://campushealth.ucr.edu/" target="_blank">Student Health Services</a> and questions about counseling records should be directed to the <a href="http://counseling.ucr.edu/" target="_blank">Counseling Center.</a></p> 
       </div> 
       <h4> <img src="/Images/square-bullet.png" alt="" /> Will I be contacted if my student is sick or hurt? What if my child is in academic trouble or facing disciplinary action?</h4> 
       <div> 
        <p>In most cases, the university will not contact you without your child's permission. In the case of an extreme emergency, where the health of your student is in serious jeopardy, or if there is a concern they pose a threat to themselves or others, the university may contact you. As a general guideline, if your child is able to communicate about the situation, it is up to them to decide if you are contacted.</p> 
       </div> 
       <h4> <img src="/Images/square-bullet.png" alt="" /> Isn't there a FERPA provision that schools can contact parents if a student violates alcohol or drug policies?</h4> 
       <div> 
        <p>FERPA regulations allow, but do not require, higher education institutions to provide notice to family when a student violates federal, state or local laws related to alcohol and/or drugs. UCR does not automatically disclose a student's alcohol and/or drug violations to family. This information may only be shared with the student’s consent, in a health or safety emergency or pursuant to another FERPA exception. Please contact the <a href="http://www.deanofstudents.ucr.edu/" target="_blank">Dean of Students</a> if you have any questions about your student's disciplinary records.</p> 
       </div> 
       <h4> <img src="/Images/square-bullet.png" alt="" /> Where can I find out more about FERPA?</h4> 
       <div> 
        <p>See the &quot;FERPA Resources&quot; box on this page for links to helpful websites and complete policies. We especially recommend <a href="http://www.ucop.edu/general-counsel/_files/ed-affairs/ferpa101.pdf" target="_blank">UC FERPA 101</a>.</p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
   </div>
